File: .\.dockerignore
General Description:
This file, .dockerignore, specifies files and directories that should be excluded from the Docker build context. It functions similarly to a .gitignore file but applies to the Docker build process, optimizing build times and reducing image sizes by preventing unnecessary files from being copied into the Docker image.


================================================================================

File: .\.gitignore
General Description:
This file is a `.gitignore` file used to specify intentionally untracked files that Git should ignore. It's designed for Visual Studio and related tools, preventing unnecessary files from being committed to a repository. It covers a wide range of temporary files, build results, user settings, and other artifacts generated by Visual Studio and its extensions.


================================================================================

File: .\.gitmodules
General Description:
This file (.gitmodules) defines Git submodules used by the project. It specifies the path and URL for the 'AerospacePropellantThermodynamics' submodule, indicating that this project incorporates code from a separate Git repository.


================================================================================

File: .\Directory.Build.props
General Description:
This file (Directory.Build.props) is a MSBuild project file used to configure build output paths for a project or solution. It defines the output directory and base intermediate output path during the build process.


================================================================================

File: .\global.json
General Description:
This file (global.json) specifies the .NET SDK version and behavior for projects referencing it. It defines the SDK version as 8.0.0, enables roll-forward to the latest major version, and allows the use of pre-release SDK versions.

File: .\projecthandler.py
General Description:
This Python script processes files within a specified directory, leveraging the Ollama API to generate descriptions and method analyses for each file. It excludes certain directories and file types (binary files).  The script takes a directory to scan and an output file path as arguments, allowing for customized analysis and results storage.

Methods:
1. def should_exclude(dirpath: str) -> bool
   - Checks if a directory should be excluded from processing based on a predefined list of excluded directory names and patterns within the directory path.
2. def get_file_description(file_path: str, file_content: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]
   - Queries the Ollama API to generate a file description in JSON format.  It formats a prompt including file type and content, sends it to Ollama, and attempts to parse the response. Handles potential JSON decode errors.
3. def process_file(file_path: str, output_file: str)
   - Processes a single file: skips large or binary files, reads content, calls get_file_description, and writes results to an output file. Handles file reading errors and attempts to use different encodings.
4. def scan_directory(root_dir: str, output_file: str)
   - Recursively scans a directory using os.walk, excluding specified directories. It then calls process_file for each file encountered.

   - Adds an image to the document, setting the page orientation and image dimensions based on the `isPortrait` flag.

   - Adds a footer to the last page of the document, with specified formatting options for the text.

   - Sets the font style (bold, underline, italic) for a given `FormattedText` object.

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\README.md
General Description:
This project performs thermodynamic optimization for combustion systems, calculating equilibrium composition and properties using thermodynamic coefficients from V.P. Glushko's work. It supports JSON input/output, mass balance, phase handling (gas and condensed), and calculates derived properties. The project includes scripts for data loading, calculations, optimization, and output.

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\src\calculators.py
General Description:
Module for thermodynamic property calculations in combustion systems, providing classes and methods for calculating properties like enthalpy, entropy, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy based on data from Glushko's work.

Methods:
1. ThermodynamicIndividualCalculator.calculate_enthalpy(coefficients: np.ndarray, temperature: float) -> float
   - Calculates molar enthalpy using thermodynamic coefficients and temperature. Converts coefficients to Joules.
2. ThermodynamicIndividualCalculator.calculate_entropy(coefficients: np.ndarray, temperature: float, partial_pressure: float = 0.0) -> float
   - Calculates molar entropy with optional pressure correction for gas-phase species. Accounts for ideal gas law.
3. ThermodynamicIndividualCalculator.calculate_heat_capacity(coefficients: np.ndarray, temperature: float) -> float
   - Calculates heat capacity using thermodynamic coefficients and temperature.
4. ThermodynamicIndividualCalculator.calculate_gibbs_energy(enthalpy: float, entropy: float, temperature: float) -> float
   - Calculates Gibbs free energy using enthalpy, entropy, and temperature.
5. ThermodynamicSystemCalculator.calculate_enthalpy(context: ThermodynamicSystemContext) -> float
   - Calculates total enthalpy of the system, summing contributions from all substances.
6. ThermodynamicSystemCalculator.calculate_entropy(context: ThermodynamicSystemContext) -> float
   - Calculates total entropy of the system, considering gas-phase and condensed-phase species.
7. ThermodynamicSystemCalculator.calculate_heat_capacity(context: ThermodynamicSystemContext) -> float
   - Calculates total heat capacity of the system, accounting for different species.
8. ThermodynamicSystemCalculator.calculate_gibbs_energy(context: ThermodynamicSystemContext) -> float
   - Calculates total Gibbs free energy of the system, summing contributions from all substances.

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\src\json_reader.py
General Description:
This module provides functions to load combustion products and input substance data from JSON files and convert them into domain objects for thermodynamic calculations. It reads data based on specific JSON structures defined for combustion products and input substances, leveraging information from "Thermodynamic and Thermophysical Properties of Combustion Products. Volume 1" by V.P. Glushko.

Methods:
1. def load_combustion_products(filepath: str) -> List[ReactionProduct]
   - Loads combustion products from a JSON file. The JSON file must contain an array of objects, each representing a reaction product with thermodynamic coefficients, phase information, and temperature range.  It creates ReactionProduct objects from the data, handling potential errors like file not found, JSON decoding issues, and missing keys.
2. def load_input_substance(filepath: str) -> PropellantComposition
   - Loads input substance data from a JSON file and returns a PropellantComposition object. The JSON file must contain an object with enthalpy and chemical composition.  It creates a PropellantComposition object and handles potential errors during file processing and data parsing.

================================================================================

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\src\json_writer.py
General Description:
This module writes thermodynamic optimization results to a JSON file, including input substance parameters, combustion products, and the resulting optimal temperature.

Methods:
1. def prepare_combustion_products(context: ThermodynamicSystemContext, filtered_products: List[ReactionProduct]) -> List[dict]:
   - Prepares a list of combustion products with their formula, phase, and moles for JSON serialization. Converts mole amounts to float to ensure correct JSON output.
2. def write_to_json(file_path: str, propellant: PropellantComposition, total_mass: float, context: ThermodynamicPropertiesContext, filtered_products: List[ReactionProduct]):
   - Writes the optimization result to a JSON file, including propellant details, calculated thermodynamic properties, and prepared combustion product data. Converts numerical values to float for JSON serialization.

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\src\main.py
General Description:
This script performs thermodynamic optimization for combustion products. It takes input propellant and combustion product data from JSON files, calculates optimal combustion temperature, and optionally writes results to an output JSON file.

Methods:
1. def main():
   - Main function that parses command-line arguments, loads data, performs temperature optimization, calculates thermodynamic properties, and optionally writes results to a JSON file. Handles errors and exits gracefully.

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\src\models.py
General Description:
This module defines data classes for representing thermodynamic equilibrium calculations in combustion processes, including temperature ranges, propellant compositions, and reaction products. It uses data from "Thermodynamic and Thermophysical Properties of Combustion Products. Volume 1" by V.P. Glushko.

Methods:
1. TemperatureRange(min: float, max: float)
   - Represents a valid temperature range for thermodynamic properties (in Kelvin).
2. PropellantComposition(enthalpy: float, composition: dict[str, float])
   - Represents the chemical composition of a rocket propellant, including enthalpy and molar quantities of elements.
3. ReactionProduct(formula: str, coefficients: list[float], phase: str, temperature_range: TemperatureRange, is_condensed: bool)
   - Represents a product species in a combustion reaction, including thermodynamic coefficients, phase, and temperature range.

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\src\optimization.py
General Description:
This module provides classes for optimizing combustion temperature and composition to achieve thermodynamic equilibrium. It minimizes Gibbs free energy while ensuring mass balance constraints.

Methods:
1. CombustionCompositionOptimizer.__init__(self, pressure: float, temperature: float, propellant_vector: np.ndarray, stoichiometric_matrix: np.ndarray, initial_guess: np.ndarray, coefficients: np.ndarray, is_condensed: np.ndarray)
   - Initializes a CombustionCompositionOptimizer object with specified parameters for combustion product composition optimization.
2. CombustionCompositionOptimizer.optimize(self) -> np.ndarray
   - Optimizes the composition of combustion products by minimizing Gibbs free energy, returning the optimized substance amounts.
3. TemperatureOptimizer.__init__(self, pressure: float, min_temperature: float, max_temperature: float, propellant: PropellantComposition, products: List[ReactionProduct])
   - Initializes a TemperatureOptimizer object with parameters for combustion temperature optimization.
4. TemperatureOptimizer.optimize(self) -> float
   - Optimizes the combustion temperature using root-finding, returning the optimal temperature.
5. TemperatureOptimizer.optimize_context_at_temperature(self, temperature: float) -> ThermodynamicSystemContext
   - Optimizes the composition of combustion products at a given temperature and returns the context.
6. TemperatureOptimizer._calculate_error(self, temperature: float) -> float
   - Calculates the error (enthalpy difference) at a given temperature for the optimization process.

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\src\thermodynamic_properties.py
General Description:
This module calculates thermodynamic properties of an optimized combustion system. It provides the `ThermodynamicPropertiesCalculator` class which computes and displays properties like total moles, condensed and gas-phase contributions, Gibbs free energy, enthalpy, entropy, and heat capacity.

Methods:
1. def __init__(self, context, filtered_products: list)
   - Constructor for the ThermodynamicPropertiesCalculator class. Initializes the calculator with a thermodynamic system context and a list of filtered products.
2. def calculate_and_display_properties(self) -> ThermodynamicPropertiesContext
   - Calculates and displays all thermodynamic properties of the optimized system, including moles, condensed/gas phase contributions, energy values, and derived quantities.  Returns a `ThermodynamicPropertiesContext` object.
3. def _calculate_weight_fraction_of_condensed_products(self) -> float
   - Calculates the total weight fraction of condensed products based on their molar mass and optimized amount.

File: .\externals\src\python\AerospacePropellantThermodynamics\src\utils.py
General Description:
This module provides utility functions for thermodynamic calculations and stoichiometric matrix construction, processing chemical formulas, filtering reaction products, and constructing matrices for thermodynamic equilibrium calculations.

Methods:
1. create_elemental_vector(propellant_composition: PropellantComposition) -> np.ndarray
   - Creates a column vector representation of element quantities from propellant composition.
2. parse_chemical_formula(formula: str) -> Dict[str, int]
   - Parses a chemical formula into its constituent elements with stoichiometric counts.
3. compute_molar_mass(elements: Dict[str, int]) -> float
   - Calculates the molar mass of a compound from its elemental composition.
4. filter_products_by_elements(reaction_products: List[ReactionProduct], propellant_composition: PropellantComposition) -> List[ReactionProduct]
   - Filters reaction products to include only those composed of elements present in the propellant.
5. construct_stoichiometric_matrix(filtered_products: List[ReactionProduct], propellant_composition: PropellantComposition) -> np.ndarray
   - Constructs a stoichiometric matrix aligned with the elements in the propellant composition.
6. filter_and_construct_matrices(reaction_products: List[ReactionProduct], propellant: PropellantComposition, temperature: float) -> Tuple[List[ReactionProduct], np.ndarray]
   - Filters products by temperature and constructs the corresponding stoichiometric matrix.
7. prepare_optimization_matrices(reaction_products: List[ReactionProduct], temperature_kelvin: float) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray, np.ndarray]
   - Prepares matrices for thermodynamic optimization, including initial guesses and condensed phase flags.
8. compute_total_mass(propellant_composition: PropellantComposition) -> float
   - Calculates the total mass of the propellant based on its composition.

File: .\src\dotnet\Apps\src\PastyPropellant.ConsoleApp\Helpers\ConstructPropellantJsonHelper.cs
General Description:
This class, `ConstructPropellantJsonHelper`, constructs a JSON file containing propellant data by combining data from JSON files and prepared propellant data. It reads propellant data from a specified file, combines it with prepared data, and generates a new JSON file with combined information.

Methods:
1. public ConstructPropellantJsonHelper(string originPropellantsFilePath, IEnumerable<PreparedPropellantData> preparedPropellantData)
   - Constructor that initializes the helper with the path to the origin propellant file and a collection of prepared propellant data.  It validates input arguments using ArgumentNullException and initializes internal data structures.
2. public async Task<OperationResult> ConstructAsync(string outputFilePath)
   - Asynchronously constructs the propellant JSON file.  It handles potential exceptions during the construction process, returning an `OperationResult` to indicate success or failure.
3. private async Task<OperationResult> TryConstructAsync(string outputFilePath)
   - Asynchronously attempts to construct the propellant JSON file. Reads propellant data, combines it with prepared data, generates the JSON, and handles errors.
4. private record ThermodynamicsJson(double Temperature, double SpecificHeatCapacity_Volume, double AverageMolarMass)
   - Represents a thermodynamics JSON object with properties for temperature, specific heat capacity, and average molar mass. Utilizes JsonPropertyName attributes for serialization/deserialization.
5. private record PorosityJson(double Porosity)
   - Represents a porosity JSON object with a porosity property. Utilizes JsonPropertyName attributes for serialization/deserialization.
6. private static T ExtractObjectFromJsonFile<T>(string filePath) where T : class
   - Extracts a JSON object from a file using the JsonSerializer.  It throws JsonException if deserialization fails.

   - Main entry point for preparing propellant data. Orchestrates the entire process, handling exceptions and returning a success or failure result.
3. private async Task<OperationResult<ReadOnlyCollection<PreparedPropellantData>>> TryPrepareAsync(string propellantsFilePath, string componentsFilePath, string combustionProductsFilePath)
   - Internal method that performs the actual data preparation steps. Calls other methods to map regions, calculate porosity, and thermodynamics properties.
4. private OperationResult<ReadOnlyCollection<ThermodynamicsPropellantResult>> RunThermodynamicsCalculator(IEnumerable<PropellantRegionMapped> regionMappeds, string combustionProductsFilePath)
   - Calculates thermodynamic properties using a Python script. Executes calculations in parallel and manages output file paths.
5. private async Task<OperationResult<ReadOnlyCollection<PorosityPropellantResult>>> RunPorosityCalculator(string propellantsFilePath, IEnumerable<PropellantRegionMapped> regionMappeds)
   - Calculates porosity using a Python script. Executes calculations asynchronously.
6. private ReadOnlyCollection<PreparedPropellantData> GetPreparedPropellantDataCollection(ReadOnlyCollection<PropellantRegionMapped> regionMappeds, ReadOnlyCollection<ThermodynamicsPropellantResult> thermodynamicsCalculatorResult, ReadOnlyCollection<PorosityPropellantResult> porosityCalculatorResult)
   - Combines the results of region mapping, thermodynamics calculation, and porosity calculation into a collection of `PreparedPropellantData`.

   - Builds a problem context matrix by doubles from the propellants data.

   - Creates and returns a collection of penalty evaluators.

   - Creates a single optimization problem context by units.

   - Creates and returns a fitness function visitor.

   - Runs the differential evolution optimization process asynchronously and returns the result.

File: .\src\dotnet\Common\src\PastyPropellant.Core\Utils\EventBus.cs
General Description:
A generic static class implementing a simple event bus pattern. It allows subscribers to register event handlers and publish events which are then delivered to all registered handlers.

Methods:
1. void Subscribe(Action<TEvent> handler)
   - Registers a new event handler to the event bus. The handler will be invoked when an event is published.
2. void Unsubscribe(Action<TEvent> handler)
   - Removes a previously registered event handler from the event bus.
3. void Publish(TEvent message)
   - Publishes an event to all registered handlers.  Each registered handler is invoked with the provided event message.

File: .\src\dotnet\ParametricCombustionModel\src\ParametricCombustionModel.Computation\Extensions\PropellantExtensions.cs
General Description:
Provides extension methods for the Propellant class to compute various parameters related to combustion, such as area volume fractions, average particle diameter, and melting/boiling temperatures.

Methods:
1. public static double GetInterPocketAreaVolumeFraction(this Propellant propellant)
   - Calculates the area volume fraction of inter-pocket regions in the propellant. Throws ArgumentNullException if Aluminum, CombustibleBinder, or AmmoniumPerchlorate components are missing.
2. public static double GetPocketAreaVolumeFraction(this Propellant propellant)
   - Calculates the area volume fraction of pocket regions in the propellant. Throws ArgumentNullException if Aluminum, CombustibleBinder, or AmmoniumPerchlorate components are missing.
3. public static double GetAverageParticlesDiameter(this Propellant propellant)
   - Gets the average particle diameter of ammonium perchlorate in the propellant. Throws ArgumentNullException if AmmoniumPerchlorate component is missing.
4. public static double GetPocketSurfaceFraction(this Propellant propellant, double pressure)
   - Calculates the pocket surface fraction based on the given pressure.
5. public static double GetMetalMeltingTemperature(this Propellant propellant)
   - Gets the metal melting temperature in Kelvins (constant value: 2300).
6. public static double GetMetalBoilingTemperature(this Propellant propellant, double pressure)
   - Calculates the metal boiling temperature based on the given pressure using a polynomial.
7. private static double GetComponentVolumeFraction(Propellant propellant, double componentMassFraction, double componentDensity)
   - Calculates the volume fraction of a component based on its mass fraction and density.
8. private static double GetCompoundMassFraction(Propellant propellant)
   - Calculates the compound mass fraction. Throws ArgumentNullException if Aluminum, CombustibleBinder, or AmmoniumPerchlorate components are missing.

General Description:
Defines an interface for objects that can be visited by a solver, enabling the application of different solvers to combustion processes using either UnitsNet types or native double values for parameters.

Methods:

   - Accepts a solver using combustion parameters based on UnitsNet types. Applies the solver to the current context using the given UnitsNet parameters.
2. void Accept(in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, ISolverVisitor solver)
   - Accepts a solver using combustion parameters based on native double values. Applies the solver to the current context using the given double parameters.

General Description:
This interface defines a visitor pattern for solving combustion problems. Solvers implementing this interface can process problem contexts, either using UnitsNet types or native double values for combustion parameters.

   - Processes a problem context using combustion solver parameters represented by UnitsNet types.
2. void Visit(in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, ProblemContextByDoubles context)
   - Processes a problem context using combustion solver parameters represented by native double values.

General Description:
Represents an abstract base class for solving kinetic propellant combustion problems. Provides methods for calculating various parameters related to the kinetic flame, such as heat flux, average temperature, density, and flame height.

Methods:
1. protected abstract void ExtractKineticBurnParams(in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits, out Frequency aKineticFlame, out MolarEnergy eKineticFlame, out double nu)
   - Extracts the kinetic flame parameters (pre-exponential factor and activation energy) from the burn parameters.
2. protected abstract void ExtractKineticBurnParams(in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, out double aKineticFlame, out double eKineticFlame, out double nu)
   - Extracts the kinetic flame parameters from burn parameters using native double types.
3. protected virtual HeatFlux GetKineticFlameHeatFlux(in Pressure pressure, in Temperature surfaceTemperature, in MassFlux decomposeRate, in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits, in KineticFlameParamsByUnits kineticFlameParamsByUnits, ref KineticFlameCombustionParams contextBag)
   - Calculates the heat flux from the kinetic flame to the propellant surface based on given parameters.
4. protected virtual Temperature GetAverageKineticFlameTemperature(in Temperature surfaceTemperature, in KineticFlameParamsByUnits kineticFlameParamsByUnits)
   - Calculates the average kinetic flame temperature.
5. protected virtual Density GetAverageKineticFlameDensity(in Pressure pressure, in Temperature averageKineticFlameTemperature, in KineticFlameParamsByUnits kineticFlameParamsByUnits)
   - Calculates the average kinetic flame density.
6. protected virtual Length GetKineticFlameHeight(in MassFlux decomposeRate, in Temperature averageKineticFlameTemperature, in Density averageKineticFlameDensity, in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits)
   - Calculates the kinetic flame height based on given parameters.

File: .\src\dotnet\ParametricCombustionModel\src\ParametricCombustionModel.Computation\Solvers\BasePropellantSolver.cs
General Description:
Represents the base class for solving propellant combustion problems in rocket engines. Provides a framework for calculating surface temperature and burn rate, defining abstract methods for derived classes to implement.

Methods:
1. void Visit(in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits, ProblemContextByUnits context)
   - Accepts a visitor to process combustion solver parameters and problem context using units. Must be implemented by derived classes.
2. protected abstract HeatFlux GetSurfaceHeatFluxesError(in Temperature surfaceTemperature, in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits, ProblemContextByUnits context)
   - Calculates the error in surface heat fluxes for the given pressure, surface temperature, and burn parameters.
3. void Visit(in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, ProblemContextByDoubles context)
   - Accepts a visitor to process combustion solver parameters and problem context using doubles. Must be implemented by derived classes.
4. protected abstract double GetSurfaceHeatFluxesError(double surfaceTemperature, in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, ProblemContextByDoubles context)
   - Calculates the error in surface heat fluxes for the given pressure, surface temperature, and burn parameters using doubles.
5. protected virtual bool TryGetSurfaceTemperature(in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits, ProblemContextByUnits context, out Temperature surfaceTemperature)
   - Attempts to find the surface temperature of the propellant using a binary search algorithm within a defined temperature range.
6. protected virtual Speed GetBurnRate(in MassFlux decomposeRate, in PropellantParamsByUnits propellantParamsByUnits)
   - Calculates the burn rate of the propellant based on the decomposition rate and propellant parameters.
7. protected virtual MassFlux GetDecomposeRate(in Temperature surfaceTemperature, in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits)
   - Calculates the decomposition rate of the propellant based on the given surface temperature and burn parameters.
8. private Temperature GetSurfaceTemperatureByBinarySearchOrFail(in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits, ProblemContextByUnits context, ref Temperature leftTemperature, ref Temperature rightTemperature, in TemperatureDelta tolerance)
   - Finds the surface temperature of the propellant using a binary search algorithm within specified temperature bounds.

General Description:
This class, InterPocketPropellantSolver, is a concrete implementation for solving kinetic propellant combustion problems specifically using the InterPocket combustion model. It handles heat flux, surface temperature, and kinetic flame parameter computations.

   - Visits a problem context, updates context with computed surface temperature, burn rate, and heat flux errors.
2. protected override HeatFlux GetSurfaceHeatFluxesError(in Temperature surfaceTemperature, in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits, ProblemContextByUnits context)
   - Calculates the error in heat fluxes by comparing kinetic flame heat flux with sublimation heat flux.

   - Extracts kinetic burn parameters (pre-exponential factor, activation energy, frequency) from provided parameters.
4. public override void Visit(in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, ProblemContextByDoubles context)
   - Visits a problem context using doubles, updates context with computed surface temperature, burn rate, and heat flux errors.  A double precision variant of the previous 'Visit' method.
5. protected override double GetSurfaceHeatFluxesError(double surfaceTemperature, in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, ProblemContextByDoubles context)
   - Calculates the error in heat fluxes by comparing kinetic flame heat flux with sublimation heat flux. A double precision variant of the previous 'GetSurfaceHeatFluxesError' method.
6. protected override void ExtractKineticBurnParams(in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, out double aKineticFlame, out double eKineticFlame, out double nu)
   - Extracts kinetic burn parameters (pre-exponential factor, activation energy, frequency) from provided parameters. A double precision variant of the previous 'ExtractKineticBurnParams' method.

General Description:
The MixedPropellantSolver class calculates combustion parameters for a mixed propellant consisting of inter-pocket and pocket propellant regions. It combines properties of these regions to determine burn rates and surface temperatures using two internal solvers, InterPocketPropellantSolver and PocketPropellantSolver.

Methods:
1. void Visit(in CombustionSolverParamsByUnits solverParamsByUnits, ProblemContextByUnits context)
   - Visits the ProblemContextByUnits with the provided CombustionSolverParamsByUnits to calculate the combustion parameters for the mixed propellant.
2. void Visit(in CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles solverParams, ProblemContextByDoubles context)
   - Visits the ProblemContextByDoubles with the provided CombustionSolverParamsByDoubles to calculate the combustion parameters for the mixed propellant.
3. Speed GetBurnRate(ProblemContextByUnits context)
   - Calculates the burn rate of the mixed propellant based on the surface temperatures of both regions and burn parameters.
4. double GetBurnRate(ProblemContextByDoubles context)
   - Calculates the burn rate of the mixed propellant based on the surface temperatures of both regions and burn parameters, returning a double value.

General Description:
BaseConstraintPenaltyEvaluator.cs: This file defines an abstract base class for constraint penalty evaluators used in optimization problems within the Parametric Combustion Model. It implements the IPenaltyEvaluator interface and provides a mechanism to apply a penalty based on constraint violations.

   - Constructor that initializes the PenaltyRate.  Throws ArgumentException if penaltyRate is not greater than 0.

   - Abstract method to calculate the penalty value based on a problem context using units. Must be implemented by derived classes.

   - Abstract method to calculate the penalty value based on a problem context using doubles. Must be implemented by derived classes.

File: .\src\dotnet\ParametricCombustionModel\src\ParametricCombustionModel.Optimization\ConstraintPenaltyEvaluators\InterPocketFasterBurnPenaltyEvaluator.cs
General Description:
This C# file defines the `InterPocketFasterBurnPenaltyEvaluator` class, which inherits from `BaseConstraintPenaltyEvaluator`. It calculates a penalty value based on the difference in burn rates between a pocket and an inter-pocket combustion zone.  The purpose is to penalize scenarios where the pocket burn rate is greater than or equal to the inter-pocket burn rate.

Methods:
1. public InterPocketFasterBurnPenaltyEvaluator(double penaltyRate)
   - Constructor for the class, initializes the penalty rate.
2. public override double GetPenaltyValue(ProblemContextByUnits updatedProblemContext)
   - Calculates the penalty value using ProblemContextByUnits. Accesses burn rates from InterPocketCombustionParams and PocketCombustionParams. Calls the private GetPenaltyValue method.
3. public override double GetPenaltyValue(ProblemContextByDoubles updatedProblemContext)
   - Calculates the penalty value using ProblemContextByDoubles. Accesses burn rates from InterPocketCombustionParams and PocketCombustionParams. Calls the private GetPenaltyValue method.
4. private double GetPenaltyValue(double pocketBurnRate, double interPocketBurnRate)
   - Calculates the penalty value based on the ratio of pocket burn rate to inter-pocket burn rate if pocket burn rate is greater than or equal to inter pocket burn rate. Otherwise, returns a zero penalty value.

   - Calculates the fitness function value using units parameters. It iterates over propellants and pressures, comparing simulated burn rates with experimental values, and returns double.MaxValue if a burn rate isn't found.

General Description:
This C# program implements a parametric combustion model optimization process. It parses command-line arguments (population size, number of generations, and input file name) to set up a Differential Evolution runtime for optimization.  It includes methods for generating populations, evaluating fitness, creating reports (text and PDF), and rendering plots of burning rates.  It also subscribes to an event bus for logging messages to the console. It defines lower and upper bounds for optimization parameters.

Methods:
1. EventBus<InfoLogEvent>.Subscribe(logEvent => { ... });
   - Subscribes to the InfoLogEvent on the event bus and prints the log message along with the sender to the console.
2. DifferentialEvolutionRuntime(populationSize, numberOfGenerations, inputFileName, lowerBound, upperBound).RunAsync()
   - Initializes and runs a Differential Evolution algorithm for optimizing parameters related to a parametric combustion model. Returns an OperationResult containing the optimization result or an exception if any occurred.
3. TextReportMaker.FromOptimizationResult(result).MakeReport()
   - Creates a text-based report from the optimization result. The report contains details of the optimization process and results.
4. BurningRatePlotRenderer().Render(operationResult, settings)
   - Renders a plot of the burning rates based on the optimization result and specified plot settings. Creates a visual representation of the burning rate behavior.
5. PdfReportMaker.FromOptimizationResult(result, pdfGeneratorAdapter).MakeReport()
   - Creates a PDF report from the optimization result and a provided PDF generator adapter.

File: .\src\dotnet\ParametricCombustionModel\src\ParametricCombustionModel.ProcessWorker\Scenarios\DifferentialEvolutionRuntime.cs
General Description:
This class implements a Differential Evolution optimization runtime for parametric combustion models. It initializes and runs the optimization process based on provided parameters, propellants, and evaluation functions.

Methods:
1. DifferentialEvolutionRuntime(int populationSize, int maxStagnationStreak, string propellantsFilePath, IEnumerable<double> lowerBound, IEnumerable<double> upperBound)
   - Constructor for the DifferentialEvolutionRuntime class. Initializes the optimizer with provided parameters, lower/upper bounds, and propellant data.  Throws an ArgumentException if lower and upper bounds have different lengths.
2. private ReadOnlyCollection<Propellant> GetPropellants(string filePath)
   - Deserializes propellant data from a JSON file.  Handles potential deserialization errors.
3. private ProblemContextByDoubles[,] GetProblemContextMatrixByDoubles(IEnumerable<Propellant> propellants)
   - Builds a problem context matrix by doubles from a collection of propellants.
4. private ProblemContextByUnits[,] GetProblemContextMatrixByUnits(IEnumerable<Propellant> propellants)
   - Builds a problem context matrix by units from a collection of propellants.
5. private IEnumerable<IPenaltyEvaluator> GetPenaltyEvaluators()
   - Creates and returns a list of penalty evaluators.  Includes heat flux ratio, burn rate, and kinetic flame heat flux penalties.
6. private OptimizationProblemContextByDoubles[] GetOptimizationProblemContextByDoubles(IEnumerable<Propellant> propellants, IEnumerable<IPenaltyEvaluator> penaltyEvaluators)
   - Creates an array of optimization problem contexts by doubles using propellants and penalty evaluators. Creates multiple contexts based on processor count.
7. private OptimizationProblemContextByUnits GetOptimizationProblemContextByUnits(ProblemContextByUnits[,] contextMatrix, IEnumerable<IPenaltyEvaluator> penaltyEvaluators)
   - Creates an optimization problem context by units using a context matrix, solver, and penalty evaluators.
8. private IFitnessFunctionVisitor GetTargetFunctionSolver()
   - Creates and returns a fitness function visitor (solver).
9. public Task<OperationResult<OptimizationResult>> RunAsync()
   - Runs the differential evolution optimization process asynchronously and returns the result.

This C# file defines the `ExecutionFrameMeasurer` class, which implements the `IExecutionFrameMeasurer` interface. It's responsible for measuring the execution time of frames within a combustion model, calculating mean and standard deviation.

Methods:
1. public ExecutionFrameMeasurer()
   - Constructor for the ExecutionFrameMeasurer class. Initializes the stopwatch and sets initial values.
2. public void StartFrame()
   - Starts the stopwatch to measure the execution time of a frame.
3. public void EndFrame()
   - Stops the stopwatch, increments the call count, updates the mean execution time, and calculates the dispersion (used for standard deviation).

File: .\src\dotnet\PastyPropellant.ConsoleApp\Controllers\Optimization\OptimizationController.cs
General Description:
This class, `OptimizationController`, is responsible for orchestrating optimization tasks using a parallel processing approach. It receives a list of optimization tasks and distributes them among worker processes, using named pipes for communication.  It handles different stopping conditions for the optimization process (iteration count or target function value boundary).

Methods:
1. OptimizationController(int processorNumber, IEnumerable<OptimizationTask> tasks)
   - Constructor that initializes the controller with the number of processor workers and a collection of optimization tasks.
2. Task<OperationResult> RunAsync()
   - Executes the optimization tasks in parallel, distributes them among worker processes, and aggregates the results.
3. Process GetRunningProcessWorker(int workerId, string pipeName, string workerPath)
   - Creates and starts a worker process for optimization, setting up arguments and preventing window creation.
4. Task<OperationResult> RunProcessWorkerAsync(int workerId, int workerNumber)
   - Runs an individual worker process, handles communication with the worker via named pipes, and manages potential exceptions.
5. Task<OperationResult<OptimizationResult>> RunIterationStopConditionAsync(OptimizationTask task, Process worker, StreamString ipcHelper)
   - Executes the optimization loop for the specified task, utilizing an iteration count-based stopping condition.
6. Task<OperationResult<OptimizationResult>> RunCrossBoundaryStopConditionAsync(OptimizationTask task, Process worker, StreamString ipcHelper)
   - Executes the optimization loop for the specified task, utilizing a target function value boundary-based stopping condition.
7. double[] GetRandomInitialPoint(ParametricModelOptimizationTicket ticket)
   - Generates a random initial point within the defined bounds for an optimization task.

File: .\src\python\RegionMapper\src\region_mappers.py
General Description:
This module defines classes responsible for mapping mass fractions of components in different regions of a propellant. Each class calculates normalized mass fractions based on input propellant and pressure (if applicable).  Classes are designed to be stateless, passing all arguments to methods.

Methods:
1. RegionData RegionData(components: Dict[str, float])
   - Data Transfer Object (DTO) for storing preprocessing calculation results. Contains a dictionary of component names and normalized mass fractions.
2. ValueError _validate_component(component: PropellantComponent, name: str)
   - Validates that a component exists and has valid properties (mass fraction within 0-1 range and not zero).
3. RegionData InterPocketRegionMapper.calculate(propellant: Propellant) -> RegionData
   - Calculates mass fractions for the inter-pocket region, which is a homogeneous mixture of all components. Mass fractions are equal to the propellant's original mass fractions.
4. RegionData PocketRegionWithoutSkeletonMapper.calculate(propellant: Propellant) -> RegionData
   - Calculates mass fractions for the pocket region without skeleton (remaining homogeneous mixture). Accounts for large particles AP.
5. RegionData PocketRegionWithSkeletonMapper.calculate(propellant: Propellant) -> RegionData
   - Calculates mass fractions for the pocket region with skeleton (binder and small AP fractions only).
6. RegionData DiffusionRegionMapper.calculate(propellant: Propellant, pressure: float) -> RegionData
   - Calculates mass fractions for the diffusion region (includes all components except agglomerated Aluminum). Takes propellant and pressure as inputs.
7. float DiffusionRegionMapper._calculate_non_agglomerated_Aluminum(al: PropellantComponent, pressure: float) -> float
   - Calculates the mass of non-agglomerated Aluminum based on the input pressure.
8. float DiffusionRegionMapper._calculate_agglomeration_fraction(coefficients: List[float], pressure: float) -> float
   - Calculates the agglomeration fraction using polynomial coefficients and pressure.

File: .\src\python\RegionMapper\src\utils.py
General Description:
This Python file (utils.py) provides utility functions for calculating molar mass, elemental composition, enthalpy, and normalizing elemental compositions.

Methods:
1. compute_molar_mass(elements: Dict[str, float]) -> float
   - Calculates the molar mass of a compound from its elemental composition. Raises KeyError if an element is not found in the molar mass database.
2. calculate_elemental_composition(region_data: Dict[str, float], component_data: Dict[str, Component]) -> Dict[str, float]
   - Calculates the overall elemental composition of a region based on mass fractions and component compositions.
3. normalize_elemental_composition(elements: Dict[str, float], propellant_molar_mass: float = 1.0) -> Dict[str, float]
   - Normalizes the elemental composition by multiplying by the molar mass of the propellant.
4. calculate_enthalpy(region_data: Dict[str, float], component_data: Dict[str, Component]) -> float
   - Calculates the overall enthalpy based on mass fractions and component enthalpies.
